from detectors.breakout import detect_breakout
from detectors.momentum import detect_momentum
from detectors.reversal import detect_reversal
from detectors.exhaustion import detect_exhaustion
from detectors.atr import detect_atr_triggers
from detectors.orderflow import detect_orderflow_triggers
from detectors.confluence import detect_confluence

def detect_all_signals(feats):
    out = []
    out += detect_breakout(feats)
    out += detect_momentum(feats)
    out += detect_reversal(feats)
    out += detect_exhaustion(feats)
    out += detect_atr_triggers(feats)
    out += detect_orderflow_triggers(feats)
    out += detect_confluence(feats)
    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/signals.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3
import logging
from datetime import datetime

DB_TRIG = "/opt/scalp/project/data/triggers.db"
DB_A    = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_SIG  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/signals.db"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename="/opt/scalp/project/logs/signals.log",
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s SIGNAL %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# DB CONNECT
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def connect(path):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# MAKE UID — STABLE UID BASED ON TS_TRIGGER
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def make_uid(instId, side, ts_trigger):
    """
    ts_trigger = UNIQUE timestamp of trigger (origin)
    → UID stable = T<ts_trigger>_<INST>_<SIDE>
    """
    clean = instId.replace("/", "")
    return f"T{ts_trigger}_{clean}_{side}"

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# LOAD TRIGGERS
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def load_triggers():
    conn = connect(DB_TRIG)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        SELECT instId, side, reason, score_B, ctx, price, atr, ts_trigger
        FROM v_triggers_latest
        ORDER BY ts_trigger DESC;
    """)
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return rows

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# LOAD CTX SCORE_A FROM A.DB
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def load_score_A():
    conn = connect(DB_A)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT instId, score_A, ctx FROM v_ctx_latest;")
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return {r[0]: (r[1], r[2]) for r in rows}

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# SAVE SIGNAL INTO SIGNALS.DB
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def save_signal(row):
    instId, side, reason, score_B, ctx_trig, price, atr, ts_trigger = row

    # score_A + ctx from a.db
    scoreA_map = load_score_A()
    score_A, ctx_A = scoreA_map.get(instId, (None, None))

    # choose ctx from triggers if available, otherwise ctx_A
    ctx = ctx_trig if ctx_trig is not None else ctx_A

    # stable UID based on ts_trigger
    trade_uid = make_uid(instId, side, ts_trigger)

    ts_local = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    hms = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")

    conn = connect(DB_SIG)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO signals
        (trade_uid, instId, side, reason, ctx,
         score_A, score_B, price, atr,
         ts_signal, ts_local, hms)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
    """, (
        trade_uid, instId, side, reason, ctx,
        score_A, score_B, price, atr,
        ts_trigger, ts_local, hms
    ))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

    logging.info(f"[SIGNAL] {trade_uid} {instId} {side} scoreB={score_B}")

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
# MAIN
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    logging.info("SIGNAL generator START")
    rows = load_triggers()
    for r in rows:
        save_signal(r)
    logging.info("SIGNAL generator DONE")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import websocket
import json
import time
import traceback

BITGET_WS = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

SUB = {
    "op": "subscribe",
    "args": [
        {
            "instType": "USDT-FUTURES",
            "channel": "books5",
            "instId": "BTCUSDT"
        }
    ]
}

def on_open(ws):
    print("WS OPEN")
    ws.send(json.dumps(SUB))
    print("Subscribed:", SUB)

def on_message(ws, msg):
    print("MSG:", msg[:500])

def on_error(ws, err):
    print("ERROR:", err)

def on_close(ws, a, b):
    print("WS CLOSED")

def main():
    while True:
        try:
            print("Connecting to", BITGET_WS)
            ws = websocket.WebSocketApp(
                BITGET_WS,
                on_open=on_open,
                on_message=on_message,
                on_error=on_error,
                on_close=on_close
            )
            ws.run_forever(ping_interval=10, ping_timeout=5)
        except Exception as e:
            print("ERR:", e)
            print(traceback.format_exc())
        time.sleep(3)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/ticks.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio
import websockets
import json
import sqlite3
import threading
import time
from queue import Queue

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_T = f"{ROOT}/data/t.db"
DB_A = f"{ROOT}/data/a.db"

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

QUEUE_MAX = 8000
FLUSH_DELAY = 0.25
ROLLING_LIMIT = 200   # nombre de ticks conservés par instrument

q = Queue(maxsize=QUEUE_MAX)
stop_event = threading.Event()

# =========================================================
# DB
# =========================================================
def conn_t():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_T, timeout=4, check_same_thread=False)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=4000;")
    return c

# =========================================================
# Symbols
# =========================================================
def load_symbols():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    L = [r[0].replace("/", "") for r in c.execute("SELECT instId FROM v_ctx_latest")]
    c.close()
    return L

# =========================================================
# Writer (rolling histo)
# =========================================================
def writer():
    conn = conn_t()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    buf = []
    last = time.time()
    print("[ticks] Writer started.")

    while not stop_event.is_set():

        # accumulate incoming ticks
        try:
            row = q.get(timeout=FLUSH_DELAY)
            buf.append(row)
        except:
            pass

        # flush
        if buf and (time.time() - last) >= FLUSH_DELAY:

            try:
                # update latest tick
                cur.executemany("""
                    INSERT INTO ticks(instId,lastPr,ts_ms)
                    VALUES (?,?,?)
                    ON CONFLICT(instId) DO UPDATE SET
                        lastPr=excluded.lastPr,
                        ts_ms=excluded.ts_ms;
                """, [(r[0], r[1], r[3]) for r in buf])

                # insert rolling history
                cur.executemany("""
                    INSERT INTO ticks_hist(instId,lastPr,ts_ms)
                    VALUES (?,?,?);
                """, [(r[0], r[1], r[3]) for r in buf])

                # enforce rolling limit per instrument
                cur.execute("""
                    DELETE FROM ticks_hist
                    WHERE id NOT IN (
                        SELECT id FROM (
                            SELECT id
                            FROM ticks_hist th
                            WHERE th.instId = ticks_hist.instId
                            ORDER BY ts_ms DESC
                            LIMIT ?
                        )
                    );
                """, (ROLLING_LIMIT,))

                conn.commit()

            except Exception as e:
                print("[ticks] DB write error:", e)
                conn.rollback()

            buf.clear()
            last = time.time()

    conn.close()

# =========================================================
# Websocket per instrument
# =========================================================
async def ws_one(instId):
    sub = {
        "op": "subscribe",
        "args": [
            {"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "ticker", "instId": instId}
        ]
    }
    msg = json.dumps(sub)

    while not stop_event.is_set():
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(
                WS_URL,
                ping_interval=10,
                ping_timeout=10,
                max_size=2**22
            ) as ws:

                await ws.send(msg)
                print(f"[ticks] {instId}: subscribed.")

                async for raw in ws:
                    data = json.loads(raw)
                    if "data" not in data:
                        continue

                    d = data["data"][0]
                    lastPr = float(d["lastPr"])
                    ts_ms = int(d["ts"])

                    if not q.full():
                        q.put((instId, lastPr, ts_ms, ts_ms))

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ticks] {instId} WS error: {e}")
            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)

# =========================================================
# MAIN
# =========================================================
def main():
    syms = load_symbols()
    print(f"[ticks] Starting {len(syms)} sockets...")

    wt = threading.Thread(target=writer, daemon=True)
    wt.start()

    try:
        asyncio.run(run_all(syms))
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        pass
    finally:
        stop_event.set()
        wt.join()

async def run_all(symbols):
    tasks = [asyncio.create_task(ws_one(s)) for s in symbols]
    await asyncio.gather(*tasks)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio
import json
import websockets

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

# Test : un seul symbole (BTCUSDT), channel = ticker
SUB_PAYLOAD = {
    "op": "subscribe",
    "args": [
        {
            "instType": "USDT-FUTURES",
            "channel": "ticker",
            "instId": "BTCUSDT"
        }
    ]
}

async def test_ws():
    print("[test] Connecting to Bitget WS...")
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=15, ping_timeout=10) as ws:
        print("[test] Connected.")

        # Send subscription
        await ws.send(json.dumps(SUB_PAYLOAD))
        print("[test] Subscription sent:", SUB_PAYLOAD)

        # Read first 20 messages
        count = 0
        async for msg in ws:
            count += 1
            print(f"[tick #{count}] {msg}")

            if count >= 20:
                print("[test] Successfully received 20 messages. WS call is OK.")
                break

async def main():
    try:
        await test_ws()
    except Exception as e:
        print("[test] ERROR:", e)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/trigger.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time, logging, traceback
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

ROOT = Path("/opt/scalp/project")

DB_TICKS   = ROOT / "data/t.db"
DB_OF      = ROOT / "data/orderflow.db"
DB_A       = ROOT / "data/a.db"
DB_U       = ROOT / "data/u.db"
DB_TRIG    = ROOT / "data/triggers.db"

LOG = ROOT / "logs/trigger.log"

FIRE_DELAY_MS = 250

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=str(LOG),
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s TRIGGER %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log = logging.getLogger("TRIGGER")

###############################################################################

def conn(db):
    c = sqlite3.connect(str(db), timeout=5)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return c

def now_ms():
    return int(time.time() * 1000)

def f(x):
    try: return float(x)
    except: return 0.0

def make_uid(inst):
    return f"H{now_ms()}_{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%H%M%S')}_{inst.replace('/','')}"

###############################################################################
# SCORES
###############################################################################

def score_orderflow(inst):
    c = conn(DB_OF)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT imbalance FROM v_orderflow_features
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts_books1 DESC LIMIT 1
    """, (inst.replace("/",""),)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return f(r[0]) if r else 0.0

def score_momentum(inst):
    c = conn(DB_TICKS)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT momentum_acc FROM v_momentum_acc
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts_ms DESC LIMIT 1
    """, (inst.replace("/",""),)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return f(r[0]) if r else 0.0

def score_breakout(inst):
    c = conn(DB_TICKS)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT pos_in_range FROM v_tick_range_position
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts_ms DESC LIMIT 1
    """, (inst.replace("/",""),)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    if not r: return 0.0
    p = f(r[0])
    if p >= 0.85: return +1.0
    if p <= 0.15: return -1.0
    return 0.0

def load_price(inst):
    c = conn(DB_TICKS)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT lastPr FROM v_ticks_latest
        WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1
    """, (inst.replace("/",""),)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return f(r[0]) if r else 0.0

def load_atr(inst):
    c = conn(DB_A)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT atr FROM feat_5m
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1
    """, (inst,)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return f(r[0]) if r else 0.0

###############################################################################
# WRITE ARMED
###############################################################################

def write_armed(row):
    c = conn(DB_TRIG)
    c.execute("""
        INSERT OR IGNORE INTO triggers (
            uid, instId, side, entry_reason,
            score_of, score_mo, score_br, score_force,
            price, atr, ts, status
        ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    """, (
        row["uid"], row["instId"], row["side"], row["entry_reason"],
        row["score_of"], row["score_mo"], row["score_br"], row["score_force"],
        row["price"], row["atr"], row["ts"], "armed"
    ))
    c.commit()
    c.close()

    log.info(
        "[ARMED] %s %s %s F=%.2f (of=%.2f mo=%.2f br=%.2f)",
        row["uid"], row["instId"], row["side"],
        row["score_force"], row["score_of"], row["score_mo"], row["score_br"]
    )

###############################################################################
# FIRE
###############################################################################

def fire_ready():
    c = conn(DB_TRIG)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT uid, ts FROM triggers
        WHERE status='armed'
    """).fetchall()

    now = now_ms()
    for r in rows:
        if now - r["ts"] >= FIRE_DELAY_MS:
            c.execute("""
                UPDATE triggers
                SET status='fire'
                WHERE uid=? AND status='armed'
            """, (r["uid"],))
            log.info("[FIRE] uid=%s", r["uid"])

    c.commit()
    c.close()

###############################################################################
# MAIN
###############################################################################

def main():
    log.info("[START] trigger running")

    while True:
        try:
            cu = conn(DB_U)
            insts = [r[0] for r in cu.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe")]
            cu.close()

            for inst in insts:
                s_of = score_orderflow(inst)
                s_mo = score_momentum(inst)
                s_br = score_breakout(inst)

                direction = s_of + s_mo + s_br
                if abs(direction) < 0.5:
                    continue

                side = "buy" if direction > 0 else "sell"

                force = abs(direction)
                if force < 0.6:
                    continue

                write_armed({
                    "uid": make_uid(inst),
                    "instId": inst,
                    "side": side,
                    "entry_reason": "ORDERFLOW+MOMENTUM+BREAKOUT",
                    "score_of": s_of,
                    "score_mo": s_mo,
                    "score_br": s_br,
                    "score_force": force,
                    "price": load_price(inst),
                    "atr": load_atr(inst),
                    "ts": now_ms()
                })

            fire_ready()

        except Exception:
            log.error("[ERR]\n%s", traceback.format_exc())

        time.sleep(0.25)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/triggers.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
# SCALP — TRIGGERS ENGINE (FULL / CLEAN / SCHEMA SAFE)

import sqlite3
import time
import logging
from pathlib import Path

###############################################################################
# PATHS
###############################################################################

ROOT = Path("/opt/scalp/project")

DB_FEAT = ROOT / "data/b.db"
DB_TICK = ROOT / "data/t.db"
DB_TRG  = ROOT / "data/triggers.db"
DB_GEST = ROOT / "data/gest.db"

LOG = ROOT / "logs/triggers.log"

###############################################################################
# CONFIG
###############################################################################

LOOP_SLEEP    = 0.01    # 10 ms
FIRE_DELAY_MS = 10      # armed -> fire

###############################################################################
# LOG
###############################################################################

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=str(LOG),
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s TRIG %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log = logging.getLogger("TRIG")

###############################################################################
# UTILS
###############################################################################

def now_ms():
    return int(time.time() * 1000)

def conn(db):
    c = sqlite3.connect(str(db), timeout=3)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=3000;")
    return c

def mk_uid(inst):
    return f"H{now_ms()}_{inst.replace('/','')}"

###############################################################################
# LOADERS
###############################################################################

def load_tick(inst):
    inst_raw = inst.replace("/", "")
    c = conn(DB_TICK)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT lastPr
        FROM v_ticks_latest
        WHERE instId=?
        LIMIT 1
    """, (inst_raw,)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return float(r["lastPr"]) if r else None

def load_feat(inst):
    c = conn(DB_FEAT)
    r = c.execute("""
        SELECT
            atr,
            mom, roc,
            ema12, ema26,
            bb_width,
            slope
        FROM feat_1m
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT 1
    """, (inst,)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return r

###############################################################################
# TRIGGERS LOGIC (PURE FUNCTIONS)
###############################################################################

def trig_momentum(f):
    if abs(f["roc"] or 0) > 0.35:
        side = "buy" if f["roc"] > 0 else "sell"
        s = min(1.0, abs(f["roc"]) / 1.0)
        return "MOMENTUM", side, 0.0, s, 0.0, s
    return None

def trig_breakout(f):
    if abs(f["slope"] or 0) > 0.0018:
        side = "buy" if f["slope"] > 0 else "sell"
        s = min(1.0, abs(f["slope"]) / 0.008)
        return "BREAKOUT", side, 0.0, 0.0, s, s
    return None

def trig_vol_expansion(f, price):
    bbw = (f["bb_width"] or 0) / price
    if bbw > 0.007:
        side = "buy" if (f["mom"] or 0) > 0 else "sell"
        s = min(1.0, bbw / 0.02)
        return "VOLATILITY_EXPANSION", side, 0.0, s, s, s
    return None

def trig_vol_squeeze(f, price):
    bbw = (f["bb_width"] or 0) / price
    if bbw < 0.002:
        side = "buy" if (f["ema12"] or 0) > (f["ema26"] or 0) else "sell"
        s = min(1.0, (0.003 - bbw) / 0.003)
        return "VOLATILITY_SQUEEZE", side, 0.0, s, 0.0, s
    return None

def trig_ema_shift(f, price):
    if f["ema12"] and f["ema26"]:
        d = (f["ema12"] - f["ema26"]) / price
        if abs(d) > 0.002:
            side = "buy" if d > 0 else "sell"
            s = min(1.0, abs(d) / 0.01)
            return "EMA_TREND_SHIFT", side, 0.0, s, 0.0, s
    return None

###############################################################################
# INSERT ARMED
###############################################################################

def insert_armed(inst, side, reason, scores, price, atr):
    uid = mk_uid(inst)
    ts = now_ms()

    c = conn(DB_TRG)
    c.execute("""
        INSERT INTO triggers (
            uid, instId, side,
            entry_reason,
            score_of, score_mo, score_br, score_force,
            price, atr,
            ts, status
        )
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?, 'armed')
    """, (
        uid,
        inst,
        side,
        reason,
        scores[0],
        scores[1],
        scores[2],
        scores[3],
        price,
        atr,
        ts
    ))
    c.commit()
    c.close()

    log.info(f"[ARMED] uid={uid} inst={inst} reason={reason} price={price}")

###############################################################################
# FIRE
###############################################################################

def fire_due():
    t = now_ms()
    c = conn(DB_TRG)

    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT uid, instId
        FROM triggers
        WHERE status='armed'
          AND (? - ts) >= ?
    """, (t, FIRE_DELAY_MS)).fetchall()

    for r in rows:
        price = load_tick(r["instId"])
        if not price:
            continue

        c.execute("""
            UPDATE triggers
            SET status='fire',
                price=?,
                ts=?
            WHERE uid=?
        """, (price, t, r["uid"]))

        if c.total_changes:
            log.info(f"[FIRE] uid={r['uid']} price={price}")

    c.commit()
    c.close()

###############################################################################
# PURGE (GEST ACK)
###############################################################################

def purge_from_gest():
    cG = conn(DB_GEST)
    uids = [r["uid"] for r in cG.execute("""
        SELECT uid FROM v_status
        WHERE status NOT IN ('armed','fire')
    """).fetchall()]
    cG.close()

    if not uids:
        return

    cT = conn(DB_TRG)
    for uid in uids:
        if cT.execute("DELETE FROM triggers WHERE uid=?", (uid,)).rowcount:
            log.info(f"[PURGE] uid={uid}")
    cT.commit()
    cT.close()

###############################################################################
# MAIN
###############################################################################

def main():
    log.info("[START] triggers engine running")

    while True:
        try:
            c = conn(DB_FEAT)
            insts = [r["instId"] for r in c.execute(
                "SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM feat_1m"
            ).fetchall()]
            c.close()

            for inst in insts:
                f = load_feat(inst)
                price = load_tick(inst)
                if not f or not price:
                    continue

                atr = f["atr"] or 0.0

                for trig in (
                    trig_momentum,
                    trig_breakout,
                    lambda x=f, p=price: trig_vol_expansion(x, p),
                    lambda x=f, p=price: trig_vol_squeeze(x, p),
                    lambda x=f, p=price: trig_ema_shift(x, p),
                ):
                    r = trig(f)
                    if not r:
                        continue

                    reason, side, so, sm, sb, sf = r
                    insert_armed(inst, side, reason, (so, sm, sb, sf), price, atr)

            fire_due()
            purge_from_gest()

        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"Loop error: {e}")

        time.sleep(LOOP_SLEEP)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/w_ticks.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time, logging, traceback

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_T = f"{ROOT}/data/t.db"
DB_TR = f"{ROOT}/data/trigger.db"
DB_WT = f"{ROOT}/data/wticks.db"

LOG = f"{ROOT}/logs/wticks.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s W-TICKS %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log = logging.getLogger("WTICKS")

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def conn(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=3, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=3000;")
    return c

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def fetch_pending_tasks():
    c = conn(DB_TR)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT uid, instId
        FROM v_wticks_tasks
        WHERE done=0;
    """).fetchall()
    c.close()
    return rows

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def get_ts_signal(uid):
    c = conn(DB_TR)
    row = c.execute("""
        SELECT ts_signal
        FROM trigger_signals
        WHERE uid=?;
    """, (uid,)).fetchone()
    c.close()
    return row[0] if row else None

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def extract_ticks(instId, ts_signal):
    ts_before = ts_signal - 10_000
    ts_after  = ts_signal + 30_000

    c = conn(DB_T)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT ts_ms, bid, ask, lastPr, vol
        FROM ticks
        WHERE instId=?
          AND ts_ms BETWEEN ? AND ?
        ORDER BY ts_ms ASC;
    """, (instId.replace("/", ""), ts_before, ts_after)).fetchall()
    c.close()

    return rows, ts_before, ts_after

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def store_ticks(uid, instId, rows, ts_signal):
    c = conn(DB_WT)

    for (ts, bid, ask, last, vol) in rows:
        window_pos = "before" if ts < ts_signal else "after"
        c.execute("""
            INSERT OR REPLACE INTO wticks
            (uid, instId, ts_ms, bid, ask, last, volume, window_pos)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?);
        """, (uid, instId, ts, bid, ask, last, vol, window_pos))

    c.close()

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def mark_done(uid):
    c = conn(DB_TR)
    c.execute("UPDATE wticks_tasks SET done=1 WHERE uid=?;", (uid,))
    c.close()

# ----------------------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    while True:
        try:
            tasks = fetch_pending_tasks()
            if not tasks:
                time.sleep(0.2)
                continue

            for uid, instId in tasks:
                log.info(f"[TASK] Processing {uid} {instId}")

                ts_signal = get_ts_signal(uid)
                if not ts_signal:
                    log.error(f"[ERR] No ts_signal for UID {uid}")
                    mark_done(uid)
                    continue

                rows, ts_before, ts_after = extract_ticks(instId, ts_signal)
                log.info(f"[TICKS] {uid} → {len(rows)} ticks found")

                store_ticks(uid, instId, rows, ts_signal)
                mark_done(uid)

        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"[ERR] main loop {e}\n{traceback.format_exc()}")
            time.sleep(0.5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/wticks.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time, logging, traceback
import statistics

ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
DB_T=f"{ROOT}/data/t.db"
DB_TR=f"{ROOT}/data/trigger.db"
DB_W=f"{ROOT}/data/wticks.db"

LOG=f"{ROOT}/logs/wticks.log"
logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s WTICKS %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log=logging.getLogger("WTICKS")

def conn(path):
    c=sqlite3.connect(path,timeout=3,isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

def fetch_tasks():
    c=conn(DB_TR)
    rows=c.execute("""
        SELECT uid, instId_raw, ts_signal, price_signal
        FROM v_wticks_tasks
        WHERE status='pending'
    """).fetchall()
    return rows

def fetch_ticks(instId_raw, ts_signal):
    c=conn(DB_T)
    t_min = ts_signal - 10_000
    t_max = ts_signal + 30_000
    rows=c.execute("""
        SELECT ts, price, bid, ask, q_buy, q_sell
        FROM ticks
        WHERE instId=? AND ts BETWEEN ? AND ?
        ORDER BY ts ASC
    """,(instId_raw, t_min, t_max)).fetchall()
    return rows

def compute_metrics(rows, price_signal, ts_signal):
    if not rows:
        return None

    prices=[r[1] for r in rows]
    ts=[r[0] for r in rows]
    minp=min(prices)
    maxp=max(prices)
    meanp=sum(prices)/len(prices)
    varp=statistics.pvariance(prices) if len(prices)>1 else 0.0

    # pic : max prix
    peak_price=maxp
    peak_ts = rows[prices.index(maxp)][0]
    delta_t = peak_ts - ts_signal
    delta_pct = (peak_price - price_signal)/price_signal if price_signal>0 else 0.0

    # pression OF simple = somme(q_buy - q_sell)
    pressure=sum([r[4]-r[5] for r in rows])

    return (peak_ts, peak_price, delta_t, delta_pct,
            minp, maxp, meanp, varp, pressure)

def save(uid, instId_raw, ts_signal, metrics):
    (peak_ts, peak_price, delta_t, delta_pct,
     minp, maxp, meanp, varp, pressure)=metrics

    ts_now=int(time.time()*1000)
    c=conn(DB_W)

    c.execute("""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO wticks_extended (
            uid, instId_raw, ts_signal,
            peak_ts, peak_price,
            delta_t_ms, delta_price_pct,
            window_min_price, window_max_price,
            window_mean_price, window_var_price,
            pressure_bias,
            ts_created, ts_updated
        )
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    """,(uid,instId_raw,ts_signal,
         peak_ts,peak_price,
         delta_t,delta_pct,
         minp,maxp,meanp,varp,
         pressure,
         ts_now,ts_now))

def mark_done(uid):
    ts=int(time.time()*1000)
    c=conn(DB_TR)
    c.execute("""
        UPDATE wticks_tasks
        SET status='done', ts_updated=?
        WHERE uid=?
    """,(ts,uid))

def main():
    while True:
        try:
            tasks=fetch_tasks()
            for uid,instId_raw,ts_signal,price_signal in tasks:
                ticks = fetch_ticks(instId_raw, ts_signal)
                metrics=compute_metrics(ticks, price_signal, ts_signal)
                if metrics:
                    save(uid,instId_raw,ts_signal,metrics)
                mark_done(uid)
                log.info(f"[DONE] WTICKS {uid}")
        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"[ERR] {e}\n{traceback.format_exc()}")

        time.sleep(0.5)

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

-- VIEWS --
v_ctx_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_latest AS
SELECT
    o.instId                         AS instId,
    o.ctx                            AS ctx,
    o.score_final                    AS score_C,
    o.ts                             AS ts_updated
FROM v_ctx_overview o
v_ctx_overview|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_overview AS
SELECT
    instId,
    DATETIME(ts_updated/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts,
    score_5m,
    score_15m,
    score_30m,
    score_final,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( exp(score_final/0.35)
                / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)), 6 )
    END AS p_buy,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( exp(-score_final/0.35)
                / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)), 6 )
    END AS p_sell,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( 1
                - (exp(score_final/0.35)
                   / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)))
                - (exp(-score_final/0.35)
                   / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35))), 6 )
    END AS p_hold,
    ctx
FROM ctx_A
ORDER BY instId
v_ohlcv_freshness|CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_freshness AS
SELECT
    instId,
    MAX(ts) AS ts,
    (strftime('%s','now') * 1000 - MAX(ts)) AS age_ms
FROM ohlcv_5m
GROUP BY instId

-- VIEWS --
v_atr_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_atr_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    CASE
        WHEN atr_signal <= 0.5 THEN 'low'
        WHEN atr_signal <= 1.5 THEN 'mid'
        ELSE 'high'
    END AS atr_bucket
FROM trades_recorded
v_ctx_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx AS ctx_dir,
    CASE
        WHEN score_A >= 0.70 THEN 'strong'
        WHEN score_A <= 0.30 THEN 'weak'
        ELSE 'mid'
    END AS score_C_bucket
FROM ctx_A
v_ctx_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_latest AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx,
    score_A AS score_C,
    ts_updated
FROM ctx_A
WHERE ts_updated = (
    SELECT MAX(ts_updated) FROM ctx_A c2 WHERE c2.instId = ctx_A.instId
)
v_historical|CREATE VIEW v_historical AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    type_signal,
    ctx,
    score_C,
    score_S,
    score_OF,
    atr_bucket,
    win_rate,
    pnl_avg,
    score_H,
    score_H AS score_H_final,
    ts_updated
FROM historical_scores
ORDER BY ts_updated DESC
v_orderflow_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_orderflow_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    CASE
        WHEN imbalance >= 0.20 THEN 'strong_buy'
        WHEN imbalance <= -0.20 THEN 'strong_sell'
        ELSE 'neutral'
    END AS of_bucket
FROM v_orderflow_features
v_score_H|CREATE VIEW v_score_H AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    ctx_dir,
    ctx_strength,
    signal_strength,
    day_bucket,
    hour_bucket,
    vol_bucket,
    of_bucket,
    total_trades,
    win_rate,
    avg_pnl,
    median_pnl,
    score_H,
    last_update
FROM historical_scores_v2
ORDER BY last_update DESC
v_scores_for_opener|CREATE VIEW v_scores_for_opener AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    ctx,
    scoreB_bucket,
    hour_bucket,
    score
FROM exposure_scores
v_signal_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_signal_bucket AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    score_B,
    CASE
        WHEN score_B >= 0.70 THEN 'strong'
        WHEN score_B <= 0.30 THEN 'weak'
        ELSE 'mid'
    END AS score_S_bucket
FROM signals_B
v_signal_timing|CREATE VIEW v_signal_timing AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    ts_signal,
    price_signal,
    peak_ts,
    peak_price,
    delta_t_ms,
    delta_price,
    delta_price_pct,
    score_T,
    ts_updated
FROM signal_timing
ORDER BY ts_updated DESC
v_timing|CREATE VIEW v_timing AS
SELECT *
FROM signal_timing
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC

-- INDEXES --
sqlite_autoindex_exposure_scores_1|
sqlite_autoindex_factor_stats_1|
sqlite_autoindex_historical_scores_1|
sqlite_autoindex_historical_scores_v2_1|
sqlite_autoindex_signal_timing_1|

0|instId|TEXT|0||0

[TABLE: budget_state]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|balance|REAL|0|1000.0|0

[TABLE: ledger]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|src|TEXT|0||0
2|instId|TEXT|0||0
3|side|TEXT|0||0
4|type|TEXT|0||0
5|amount|REAL|0||0
6|ts|INTEGER|0|strftime('%s','now')*1000|0

[TABLE: v_budget_overview]
0|balance||0||0
1|margin||0||0
2|pnl_real||0||0
3|last_update||0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_balance|CREATE VIEW v_balance AS
SELECT balance_usdt
FROM balance
WHERE id = 1
v_budget_overview|CREATE VIEW v_budget_overview AS
SELECT
  ROUND(balance,6) AS balance,
  ROUND(margin,6)  AS margin,
  ROUND(pnl_real,6) AS pnl_real,
  datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM budget_state
v_exposure|CREATE VIEW v_exposure AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='margin' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS margin,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='pnl_real' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS pnl_real
FROM ledger
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY ABS(margin) DESC

-- INDEXES --
idx_bus_out_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack)
idx_bus_out_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ts ON bus_out(ts)

    uid,

v_active_coins|CREATE VIEW v_active_coins AS
SELECT DISTINCT
    instId
FROM gest
WHERE status IN (
    'armed',
    'fire',
    'opened',
    'follow',
    'to_close'
)
AND instId IS NOT NULL
v_gest|CREATE VIEW v_gest AS
SELECT *
FROM gest
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
v_gest_status_count|CREATE VIEW v_gest_status_count AS
SELECT
    status,
    COUNT(*) AS cnt
FROM gest
GROUP BY status
v_status|CREATE VIEW v_status AS
SELECT
    uid,
    status
FROM gest

SELECT *
FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE ts IN (
    SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_15m AS o2
    WHERE o2.instId = ohlcv_15m.instId
    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT 150
)

FROM ohlcv_30m

)

-- VIEWS --
v_orderflow_features|CREATE VIEW v_orderflow_features AS
WITH
    last_b1 AS (
        SELECT b.*
        FROM books1 b
        JOIN (
            SELECT instId, MAX(ts_ms) AS max_ts
            FROM books1
            WHERE ts_ms IS NOT NULL
            GROUP BY instId
        ) t
        ON b.instId = t.instId AND b.ts_ms = t.max_ts
    ),
    last_b5 AS (
        SELECT b.*
        FROM books5 b
        JOIN (
            SELECT instId, MAX(ts_ms) AS max_ts
            FROM books5
            WHERE ts_ms IS NOT NULL
            GROUP BY instId
        ) t
        ON b.instId = t.instId AND b.ts_ms = t.max_ts
    )

SELECT
    b1.instId,

    -- timestamps
    b1.ts_ms     AS ts_books1,
    b5.ts_ms     AS ts_books5,

    -- best prices
    b1.best_bid,
    b1.best_ask,

    -- micro sizes
    b1.bid_size,
    b1.ask_size,
    b1.imbalance,

    -- depth 5
    b5.mid,
    b5.spread,
    b5.bid1, b5.bid2, b5.bid3,
    b5.ask1, b5.ask2, b5.ask3,
    b5.wall_bid,
    b5.wall_ask,

    -- derived features
    (b5.wall_bid - b5.wall_ask) AS wall_diff,
    CASE WHEN (b5.wall_bid + b5.wall_ask) > 0
        THEN (b5.wall_bid - b5.wall_ask) * 1.0
             / (b5.wall_bid + b5.wall_ask)
        ELSE NULL
    END AS wall_ratio

FROM last_b1 b1
LEFT JOIN last_b5 b5 USING(instId)
ORDER BY b1.instId

-- INDEXES --
idx_b15_inst|CREATE INDEX idx_b15_inst ON books15(instId, ts_ms)
idx_b15_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_b15_ts ON books15(ts_ms)
sqlite_autoindex_meta_1|

27|fee_total|REAL|0||0
28|score_of|REAL|0||0
29|score_mo|REAL|0||0
30|score_br|REAL|0||0
31|score_force|REAL|0||0
32|dominant_detector||0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_recorder|CREATE VIEW v_recorder AS
SELECT
    uid,
    ts_recorded
FROM recorder
v_recorder_dominant_detector|CREATE VIEW v_recorder_dominant_detector AS
SELECT *,
CASE
    WHEN score_of >= score_mo AND score_of >= score_br THEN 'ORDERFLOW'
    WHEN score_mo >= score_of AND score_mo >= score_br THEN 'MOMENTUM'
    WHEN score_br >= score_of AND score_br >= score_mo THEN 'BREAKOUT'
    ELSE 'MIXED'
END AS dominant_detector
FROM recorder
v_recorder_duration|CREATE VIEW v_recorder_duration AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    entry,
    price_close,
    pnl,
    pnl_pct,
    pnl_net,
    reason_close,
    ts_open,
    ts_close,
    (ts_close - ts_open) / 1000.0 AS dur_s,

    CASE
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 500 THEN '0–0.5s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 1000 THEN '0.5–1s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 3000 THEN '1–3s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 5000 THEN '3–5s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 10000 THEN '5–10s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 30000 THEN '10–30s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 60000 THEN '30–60s'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 120000 THEN '1–2m'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 300000 THEN '2–5m'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 600000 THEN '5–10m'
        WHEN (ts_close - ts_open) < 1800000 THEN '10–30m'
        ELSE '>30m'
    END AS dur_bucket,

    CASE WHEN pnl > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS is_win,
    CASE WHEN pnl < 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS is_loss
FROM recorder
WHERE ts_open IS NOT NULL
  AND ts_close IS NOT NULL
v_recorder_for_gest|CREATE VIEW v_recorder_for_gest AS
SELECT
  uid, status, ts_record
FROM trades_record
WHERE status='recorded'
ORDER BY ts_record DESC
v_recorder_score_ranges|CREATE VIEW v_recorder_score_ranges AS
SELECT *,
CASE
    WHEN score_force < 0.6 THEN '<0.6'
    WHEN score_force < 0.7 THEN '0.6-0.7'
    WHEN score_force < 0.8 THEN '0.7-0.8'
    ELSE '>0.8'
END AS force_bucket
FROM recorder
v_recorder_stats_by_duration|CREATE VIEW v_recorder_stats_by_duration AS
SELECT
    dur_bucket,
    COUNT(*) AS trades,
    SUM(is_win) AS wins,
    SUM(is_loss) AS losses,
    ROUND(100.0 * SUM(is_win) / COUNT(*), 2) AS winrate_pct,
    ROUND(SUM(pnl), 6) AS pnl_total,
    ROUND(AVG(pnl), 6) AS pnl_avg,
    ROUND(AVG(pnl_pct), 4) AS pct_avg,
    ROUND(AVG(dur_s), 3) AS dur_avg_s
FROM v_recorder_duration
GROUP BY dur_bucket
ORDER BY dur_avg_s
v_trades_analyse|CREATE VIEW v_trades_analyse AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    reason AS reason_signal,
    reason_close,
    price_signal,
    atr_signal,
    score_A,
    score_B,
    ts_open,
    ts_close,
    entry,
    price_close,
    sl_init,
    tp_init,
    sl_be,
    sl_trail,
    tp_dyn,
    price_to_close,
    pnl
FROM trades_record
ORDER BY ts_open ASC

-- INDEXES --
idx_rec_inst|CREATE INDEX idx_rec_inst  ON trades_recorded(instId)
idx_rec_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_rec_ts    ON trades_recorded(ts_close)
idx_rec_uid|CREATE INDEX idx_rec_uid   ON trades_recorded(uid)
idx_recorder_uid|CREATE INDEX idx_recorder_uid
    ON recorder(uid)
sqlite_autoindex_recorder_1|
sqlite_autoindex_records_1|
sqlite_autoindex_trades_record_1|
sqlite_autoindex_trades_recorded_1|

0|uid|TEXT|0||0

3|reason|TEXT|0||0
4|ctx|TEXT|0||0
5|score_A|REAL|0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_for_gest|CREATE VIEW v_for_gest AS
SELECT
    s.trade_uid AS uid,
    s.instId,
    s.side,
    s.reason,
    s.ctx,
    s.score_A,
    s.score_B,
    s.price AS price_signal,
    s.atr   AS atr_signal,
    s.ts_signal
FROM signals s
JOIN (
    SELECT instId, MAX(ts_signal) AS max_ts
    FROM signals
    GROUP BY instId
) x ON x.instId = s.instId
   AND x.max_ts = s.ts_signal
ORDER BY s.ts_signal DESC

-- INDEXES --
sqlite_autoindex_signals_1|

3|ts_ms|INTEGER|1||0

[TABLE: v_hist_ordered]

2|ts_ms|INTEGER|0||0
3|rn||0||0

[TABLE: v_tick_range]

[TABLE: v_momentum_1]
0|instId|TEXT|0||0
1|lastPr|REAL|0||0
2|momentum_1||0||0
3|ts_ms|INTEGER|0||0

[TABLE: v_tick_range_position]
0|instId|TEXT|0||0
1|lastPr|REAL|0||0
2|ts_ms|INTEGER|0||0
3|pos_in_range||0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_atr|CREATE VIEW v_atr AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    -- fast ATR (10)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 10) AS atr_fast,

    -- slow ATR (30)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 30) AS atr_slow
FROM v_ticks_latest l
v_hist_ordered|CREATE VIEW v_hist_ordered AS
SELECT
    h.instId,
    h.lastPr,
    h.ts_ms,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
        PARTITION BY h.instId
        ORDER BY h.ts_ms DESC
    ) AS rn
FROM ticks_hist h
v_momentum_1|CREATE VIEW v_momentum_1 AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    (l.lastPr - h.lastPr) AS momentum_1,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_hist_ordered h
    ON h.instId = l.instId AND h.rn = 1
v_momentum_acc|CREATE VIEW v_momentum_acc AS
SELECT
    m.instId,
    m.ts_ms,
    (
        SELECT SUM(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr)
        FROM v_hist_ordered h2
        JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
            ON h3.instId = h2.instId
           AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
        WHERE h2.instId = m.instId
        AND h2.rn <= 10
    ) AS momentum_acc
FROM v_momentum_1 m
v_momentum_debug|CREATE VIEW v_momentum_debug AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ts_ms,
    momentum_acc
FROM v_momentum_acc
ORDER BY ts_ms DESC
v_tick_classifier|CREATE VIEW v_tick_classifier AS
SELECT
    a.instId,
    CASE
        WHEN a.atr_fast IS NULL THEN 'NEUTRAL'
        WHEN a.atr_fast > a.atr_slow * 1.8 THEN 'BREAKOUT'
        WHEN a.atr_fast < a.atr_slow * 0.4 THEN 'SQUEEZE'
        ELSE 'CHOP'
    END AS class_signal
FROM v_atr a
v_tick_range|CREATE VIEW v_tick_range AS
SELECT instId,
       ABS(lastPr - prevPr) AS tr,
       ts_ms
FROM v_hist_ordered
WHERE prevPr IS NOT NULL
v_tick_range_position|CREATE VIEW v_tick_range_position AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr,ts_ms,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) rn
    FROM ticks_hist
),
range_win AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr FROM base WHERE rn <= 26
),
agg AS (
    SELECT instId, MIN(lastPr) AS minP, MAX(lastPr) AS maxP
    FROM range_win GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
   t.instId,
   t.lastPr,
   t.ts_ms,
   CASE WHEN a.maxP = a.minP THEN 0.5
        ELSE (t.lastPr - a.minP)/(a.maxP - a.minP)
   END AS pos_in_range
FROM ticks t
JOIN agg a USING(instId)
v_tick_volatility|CREATE VIEW v_tick_volatility AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts_ms,
        ABS(lastPr - LAG(lastPr) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms)) AS tr,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) AS rn
    FROM ticks_hist
)
SELECT
    instId,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 11 THEN tr END) AS atr_fast,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 26 THEN tr END) AS atr_slow
FROM base
GROUP BY instId
v_ticks_for_follower|CREATE VIEW v_ticks_for_follower AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    m1.momentum_1,
    COALESCE(macc.momentum_acc, 0) AS momentum_acc,
    a.atr_fast,
    a.atr_slow,
    0 AS pos_in_range,           -- volontairement ignoré (non utilisé)
    c.class_signal,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_1 m1 ON m1.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_acc macc ON macc.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_atr a ON a.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_tick_classifier c ON c.instId = l.instId
v_ticks_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.lastPr,
    t.ts_ms
FROM ticks t

-- INDEXES --
idx_hist_inst_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_hist_inst_ts ON ticks_hist(instId, ts_ms DESC)
sqlite_autoindex_ticks_1|

3|bid|REAL|0||0
4|ask|REAL|0||0
5|last|REAL|0||0
6|volume|REAL|0||0
7|window_pos|TEXT|1||0

[TABLE: wticks_extended]
0|uid|TEXT|0||1
1|instId_raw|TEXT|0||0
2|ts_signal|INTEGER|0||0
3|peak_ts|INTEGER|0||0
4|peak_price|REAL|0||0
5|delta_t_ms|INTEGER|0||0
6|delta_price_pct|REAL|0||0
7|window_min_price|REAL|0||0
8|window_max_price|REAL|0||0
9|window_mean_price|REAL|0||0
10|window_var_price|REAL|0||0
11|pressure_bias|REAL|0||0
12|ts_created|INTEGER|0||0
13|ts_updated|INTEGER|0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_wticks|CREATE VIEW v_wticks AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    ts_ms,
    bid,
    ask,
    last,
    volume,
    window_pos
FROM wticks
ORDER BY uid, ts_ms
v_wticks_extended|CREATE VIEW v_wticks_extended AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId_raw,
    ts_signal,
    peak_ts,
    peak_price,
    delta_t_ms,
    delta_price_pct,
    window_min_price,
    window_max_price,
    window_mean_price,
    window_var_price,
    pressure_bias,
    ts_created,
    ts_updated
FROM wticks_extended
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC

-- INDEXES --
idx_wt_uid|CREATE INDEX idx_wt_uid ON wticks_extended(uid)
idx_wticks_inst|CREATE INDEX idx_wticks_inst ON wticks(instId)
idx_wticks_uid|CREATE INDEX idx_wticks_uid ON wticks(uid)
sqlite_autoindex_wticks_1|
sqlite_autoindex_wticks_extended_1|
